The range of those participating included many different denominations such as Anglicans, Assemblies of God, Baptist, Christian Reformed, Lutheran and Presbyterian.\r\n\r\nThe NIV is a balance between word-for-word and thought-for-thought or literal and phrase by phrase translations.\r\n\r\nRecent archaeological and linguistic discoveries helped in understanding passages that have traditionally been difficult to translate.
